        /**

         * Remove Nulls return '' || underfined || obj

         */

        function removeNulls(obj) {

            if (typeof obj === 'undefined') {

                return undefined;

            }

            if (obj === null) {

                return '';

            }

            if (typeof obj === 'object') {

                for (let key in obj) {

                    obj[key] = removeNulls(obj[key]);

                }

            }

            return obj;

        }



        function searchProductDataById(id, arrayProduct) {

            for (let i in arrayProduct) {

                for (let k in arrayProduct[i]) {

                    if (k == id) {

                        return arrayProduct[i][k];

                    }

                }

            }

            return null;

        }



        function getValuesFromArray(array) {

            let arrayValues = [];

            for (let i in array) {

                for (let k in array[i]) {

                    if (!isNaN(k)) {

                        arrayValues.push(array[i][k]);

                    }

                }

            }

            return arrayValues;

        }



        function removeEvent(obj, value) {

            for (var index in obj) {

                if (obj[index].hasOwnProperty('event') && obj[index]['event'] == value) {

                    delete obj[index];

                }

            }

        }



        function getCurrencyCode() {

            let currencyCode = "USD";

            return removeNulls(currencyCode);

        }



        function getCurrencySymbol() {

            let currencySymbol = "$";

            return removeNulls(currencySymbol);

        }



        function shippingOption() {

            let option = null;

            return removeNulls(option);

        }



        function getCheckoutOption() {

            let option = null;

            return removeNulls(option);

        }



        function getProductCart() {

            let productCart = {"products":[{"89121":{"id":"MA88HAEP","name":"EGENC62378705","price":"1605.00","brand":false,"category":false,"variant":"","quantity":"5.00","dimension124":"undefined","dimension125":"undefined","dimension126":"MA72HAEP.CD1JAWR","dimension127":"28 p\u1d9f |French Door |Slim SpacePlus\u2122 |Compresor linear inverter |Acero Inoxidable |ThinQ\u2122 (Neto: 26 p\u1d9f)"}}],"label":"MA88HAEP"};

        function changeQtyWishlist(e, id) {

            let qty = e.options[e.selectedIndex].text;

            localStorage.setItem('qtyProductWishlist-' + id, parseInt(qty));

        }



        function eventAddToCart(id) {

            setCookieGa('checkout1', false);

            setCookieGa('checkout2', false);

            let qty = localStorage.getItem('qtyProductWishlist-' + id);

            let productsWishlist = null;

            let products = searchProductDataById(id, productsWishlist.products);

            if (qty) {

                products.quantity = parseInt(qty);

                localStorage.removeItem('qtyProductWishlist-' + id);

            }



            let productsInfo = {

                'event': 'addToCart',

                'label': products.id,

                'siteType': 'B2C',

                'pagePurpose': 'obs',

                'ecommerce': {

                    'currencyCode': getCurrencyCode(),

                    'add': {

                        'products': products

                    }

                }

            };

            localStorage.setItem('productData', JSON.stringify(productsInfo));

            console.log('productid: ' + products.id);

            javascript:window.ta && ta.ClickTrack(this, 100001, 'LG|add_to_cart', {

                'itms': [

                    {productid: products.id}

                ]

            });

        }



        function removeItem(id) {

            setCookieGa('checkout1', false);

            setCookieGa('checkout2', false);

            setCookieGa('checkout21', false);

            setCookieGa('_dl', false);

            let productsCart = getProductCart();

            let products = searchProductDataById(id, productsCart.products);

            let productsInfo = {

                'event': 'removeCart',

                'label': products.id,

                'siteType': 'B2C',

                'pagePurpose': 'obs',

                'ecommerce': {

                    'currencyCode': getCurrencyCode(),

                    'remove': {

                        'products': [products]

                    }

                }

            };

            localStorage.setItem('productData', JSON.stringify(productsInfo));

        }

            console.log('console.log(standardData): ', window.standardData);

            console.log('console.log(dataLayer): ', window.dataLayer);

            console.log('----------------------------END GOOGLE ANALYTICS DATA------------------------');

        }



        function checkout1Page() {

            if (getCookieGa('checkout1') == "true" || getCookieGa('checkout2') == "true") {

                return;

            }

            let event = 'checkout1';

            setCookieGa('checkout1', true);

            let productsCart = getProductCart();

            let productsInfo = {

                'event': event,

                'label': productsCart.label,

                'siteType': 'B2C',

                'pagePurpose': 'obs',

                'ecommerce': {

                    'currencyCode': getCurrencyCode(),

                    'checkout': {

                        'actionField': {

                            'action': 'checkout',

                            'step': 1

                        },

                        'products': getValuesFromArray(productsCart.products)

                    }

                }

            };

            dataLayer.push(removeNulls(productsInfo));

            console.log('---------------Begin checkout1Page --------------');

            gtmLog();

            console.log('---------------End checkout1Page ----------------');

        }

        function checkEventExists(event) {

            for (let index in dataLayer) {

                if (dataLayer.hasOwnProperty(index)

                    && dataLayer[index].hasOwnProperty('event')

                    && dataLayer[index]['event'] === event

                ) {

                    return true;

                }

            }

            return false;

        }



        window.onpopstate = function (event) {

            if (window.location.href.indexOf('#shipping') > 0 && !checkEventExists('checkout2')) {

                checkout1Page();

            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('#payment') > 0 && !checkEventExists('checkout2')) {

                checkoutPage2();

            }

        };



        /**

         * Tracking for checkout shipping

         */



        var onePageCheckoutStores = ["de", "uk", "cac_en", "ch_de", "eg_en", "fr", "cl", "mx", "pe"];

        var isSuccessPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/onepage/success') > 0 || window.location.href.indexOf('/banktransfer/page/success') > 0;

        var isCartPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/cart') > 0;

        var isCheckoutPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/') > 0 && !isCartPage;

        var isShippingPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/#shipping') > 0;

        var isPaymentPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/#payment') > 0;

        var isFailurePage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/onepage/failure') > 0;

        var isEnhancedPurchase = "0";



        if (isCartPage) {

            setCookieGa('checkout1', false);

            setCookieGa('checkout2', false);

            setCookieGa('checkout21', false);

        }

        if (isSuccessPage) {

            setCookieGa('_dl', false);

            if (isEnhancedPurchase == 1) {

                successPageEnhanced();

            } else {

                successPage();

            }

        } else {

            var storeCode = "cac_en";

            if (isShippingPage || (onePageCheckoutStores.includes(storeCode) && isCheckoutPage && !isFailurePage)) {

                checkout1Page();

            } else if (isPaymentPage) {

                checkoutPage2();

            }

        }



        

        function getCookieGa(cname) {

            let name = cname + "=";

            let decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);

            let ca = decodedCookie.split(';');

            for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {

                let c = ca[i];

                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {

                    c = c.substring(1);

                }

                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {

                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);

                }

            }

            return '';

        }



        

        function setCookieGa(cname, cvalue) {

            const d = new Date();

            d.setTime(d.getTime() + 1800000);

            let expires = 'expires=' + d.toUTCString();

            document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';' + expires + ';path=/';

        }</script>

        function setCookieLocalTime() {

            var currentTime = new Date();

            var hours = currentTime.getHours();

            var minutes = currentTime.getMinutes();

            var year = currentTime.getFullYear();

            var mouth = currentTime.getMonth() + 1;

            var date = currentTime.getDate();

            var sec = currentTime.getSeconds();



            var suffix = "AM";



            if (hours >= 12) {

                suffix = "PM";

                hours;

            }



            if (hours == 0) {

                hours = 12;

            }



            if (minutes < 10) {

                minutes = "0" + minutes;

            }



            if (sec < 10) {

                sec = "0" + sec;

            }



            

            const tz = Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone;



            currentTime.setTime(currentTime.getTime()+(60*1000));

            document.cookie="time_client_date="+year+"-"+mouth+"-"+date+" "+hours +":"+minutes+":"+ sec +";path=/";

            document.cookie="time_zone_client="+tz +";path=/";

        }</script>
